##ID_225## tempo: 45 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
service-name: OperacaoProducaoSP.criarApontamento
uri: /mgeprod/service.sbr
*/
SELECT TPRIPA.CODPRODPA AS CODPRODPA,TPRIPA.CONCLUIDO AS CONCLUIDO,TPRIPA.CONTROLEPA AS CONTROLEPA,TPRIPA.DTFAB AS DTFAB,TPRIPA.DTVAL AS DTVAL,TPRIPA.IDIPROC AS IDIPROC,TPRIPA.NROLOTE AS NROLOTE,TPRIPA.QTDPRODUZIR AS QTDPRODUZIR,TPRIPA.QTDPRODUZIR_ORIGINAL AS QTDPRODUZIR_ORIGINAL, ( SELECT REFERENCIA FROM TGFPRO PRO WHERE CODPROD = TPRIPA.CODPRODPA) AS REFERENCIA, ( 
	SELECT
		  TPRIPA.QTDPRODUZIR - NVL(SUM(NOTA.QTDNEG), 0) - (CASE
                                                       				WHEN NVL(SUM(NOTA.QTDNEG), 0) > 0 THEN NVL(MAX(APO_PERDA.QTDPERDA), 0)
                                                      				ELSE 0 
                                                      			  END) AS SALDO
	FROM
		TPRIPA IPA
	INNER JOIN TPRIPROC IPROC ON (IPA.IDIPROC = IPROC.IDIPROC)
	LEFT JOIN (
		SELECT IDIPROC, ITE.QTDNEG, ITE.CODPROD, ITE.CONTROLE 
		FROM TGFCAB CAB INNER JOIN TGFITE ITE ON (ITE.NUNOTA = CAB.NUNOTA)
						INNER JOIN TPRROPE ROPE ON (ROPE.NUNOTA = CAB.NUNOTA)
						INNER JOIN TPROEST OEST ON (OEST.IDEFX = ROPE.IDEFX AND OEST.SEQOPER = ROPE.SEQOPER)
		WHERE CAB.IDIPROC IS NOT NULL 
			AND OEST.TIPOITENS = 'PA'
			AND OEST.QUANDO = 'PA'
			AND CAB.TIPMOV = 'F'
	) NOTA ON (NOTA.IDIPROC = IPROC.IDIPROC AND NOTA.CODPROD = IPA.CODPRODPA AND (NVL(NOTA.CONTROLE, ' ') = ' ' OR NVL(NOTA.CONTROLE, ' ') = NVL(IPA.CONTROLEPA, ' ')))
	LEFT JOIN (
		SELECT  NVL(SUM(APA.QTDPERDA), 0) AS QTDPERDA , IATV.IDIPROC, APA.CODPRODPA, APA.CONTROLEPA
   		FROM TPRAPA APA
   		INNER JOIN TPRAPO APO ON(APO.NUAPO = APA.NUAPO)
   		INNER JOIN TPRIATV IATV ON(IATV.IDIATV = APO.IDIATV)
   		WHERE APO.SITUACAO = 'C'
   			AND APA.QTDPERDA > 0
		GROUP BY IATV.IDIPROC, APA.CODPRODPA, APA.CONTROLEPA
	) APO_PERDA ON (APO_PERDA.IDIPROC = IPROC.IDIPROC AND APO_PERDA.CODPRODPA = IPA.CODPRODPA AND (NVL(APO_PERDA.CONTROLEPA, ' ') = ' ' OR NVL(APO_PERDA.CONTROLEPA, ' ') = NVL(IPA.CONTROLEPA, ' ')))
	WHERE IPA.CODPRODPA = TPRIPA.CODPRODPA
		AND NVL(IPA.CONTROLEPA, ' ') = TPRIPA.CONTROLEPA
		AND IPROC.STATUSPROC IN ('A', 'R', 'P2', 'S', 'S2')
		AND IPROC.IDIPROC = TPRIPA.IDIPROC) AS SALDOOP FROM TPRIPA /*SQL_92_JOINED_TABLES*/   WHERE (TPRIPA.IDIPROC = ?) 
Params:
  1 = 12356
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
##ID_226## tempo: 46 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
service-name: OperacaoProducaoSP.criarApontamento
uri: /mgeprod/service.sbr
*/
SELECT TPRIPA.CODPRODPA AS CODPRODPA,TPRIPA.CONCLUIDO AS CONCLUIDO,TPRIPA.CONTROLEPA AS CONTROLEPA,TPRIPA.DTFAB AS DTFAB,TPRIPA.DTVAL AS DTVAL,TPRIPA.IDIPROC AS IDIPROC,TPRIPA.NROLOTE AS NROLOTE,TPRIPA.QTDPRODUZIR AS QTDPRODUZIR,TPRIPA.QTDPRODUZIR_ORIGINAL AS QTDPRODUZIR_ORIGINAL, ( SELECT REFERENCIA FROM TGFPRO PRO WHERE CODPROD = TPRIPA.CODPRODPA) AS REFERENCIA, ( 
	SELECT
		  TPRIPA.QTDPRODUZIR - NVL(SUM(NOTA.QTDNEG), 0) - (CASE
                                                       				WHEN NVL(SUM(NOTA.QTDNEG), 0) > 0 THEN NVL(MAX(APO_PERDA.QTDPERDA), 0)
                                                      				ELSE 0 
                                                      			  END) AS SALDO
	FROM
		TPRIPA IPA
	INNER JOIN TPRIPROC IPROC ON (IPA.IDIPROC = IPROC.IDIPROC)
	LEFT JOIN (
		SELECT IDIPROC, ITE.QTDNEG, ITE.CODPROD, ITE.CONTROLE 
		FROM TGFCAB CAB INNER JOIN TGFITE ITE ON (ITE.NUNOTA = CAB.NUNOTA)
						INNER JOIN TPRROPE ROPE ON (ROPE.NUNOTA = CAB.NUNOTA)
						INNER JOIN TPROEST OEST ON (OEST.IDEFX = ROPE.IDEFX AND OEST.SEQOPER = ROPE.SEQOPER)
		WHERE CAB.IDIPROC IS NOT NULL 
			AND OEST.TIPOITENS = 'PA'
			AND OEST.QUANDO = 'PA'
			AND CAB.TIPMOV = 'F'
	) NOTA ON (NOTA.IDIPROC = IPROC.IDIPROC AND NOTA.CODPROD = IPA.CODPRODPA AND (NVL(NOTA.CONTROLE, ' ') = ' ' OR NVL(NOTA.CONTROLE, ' ') = NVL(IPA.CONTROLEPA, ' ')))
	LEFT JOIN (
		SELECT  NVL(SUM(APA.QTDPERDA), 0) AS QTDPERDA , IATV.IDIPROC, APA.CODPRODPA, APA.CONTROLEPA
   		FROM TPRAPA APA
   		INNER JOIN TPRAPO APO ON(APO.NUAPO = APA.NUAPO)
   		INNER JOIN TPRIATV IATV ON(IATV.IDIATV = APO.IDIATV)
   		WHERE APO.SITUACAO = 'C'
   			AND APA.QTDPERDA > 0
		GROUP BY IATV.IDIPROC, APA.CODPRODPA, APA.CONTROLEPA
	) APO_PERDA ON (APO_PERDA.IDIPROC = IPROC.IDIPROC AND APO_PERDA.CODPRODPA = IPA.CODPRODPA AND (NVL(APO_PERDA.CONTROLEPA, ' ') = ' ' OR NVL(APO_PERDA.CONTROLEPA, ' ') = NVL(IPA.CONTROLEPA, ' ')))
	WHERE IPA.CODPRODPA = TPRIPA.CODPRODPA
		AND NVL(IPA.CONTROLEPA, ' ') = TPRIPA.CONTROLEPA
		AND IPROC.STATUSPROC IN ('A', 'R', 'P2', 'S', 'S2')
		AND IPROC.IDIPROC = TPRIPA.IDIPROC) AS SALDOOP FROM TPRIPA /*SQL_92_JOINED_TABLES*/   WHERE ( TPRIPA.IDIPROC = ? AND TPRIPA.CONCLUIDO = 'N')  AND ROWNUM <= 501
Params:
  1 = 12356

##ID_813## tempo: 1 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
entity: InstanciaAtividade
service-name: DatasetSP.loadRecords
uri: /mge/service.sbr
*/
 SELECT 
X.*
FROM( 
	SELECT
	    
		IPA.CODPRODPA,
	 	IPA.NROLOTE,
		IPA.CONTROLEPA,
		IPA.QTDPRODUZIR,
		PRO.COMPLDESC,
		PRO.CODVOL,
		PRO.CODGRUPOPROD,
		PRO.DESCRPROD,
		MPS.DTINICMPS,
		MPS.DTFINMPS,
		PRO.DECQTD,
		PRO.REFERENCIA,
		GRU.DESCRGRUPOPROD,
		IPROC.PRIORIDADE  AS PRIORIDADE,
		(SELECT COUNT(1) FROM TPRIPA IPA3 WHERE IPA3.IDIPROC = IPA.IDIPROC) AS QTDPRODUTOS,
		(CASE WHEN IPA.NROLOTE <> 'CURINGA' THEN 1 ELSE 2 END) AS ORDER_NROLOTE
	FROM
		TPRIPA IPA INNER JOIN TGFPRO PRO ON(IPA.CODPRODPA = PRO.CODPROD)
		INNER JOIN TPRIPROC IPROC ON(IPROC.IDIPROC = IPA.IDIPROC)
		INNER JOIN TGFGRU GRU ON(PRO.CODGRUPOPROD = GRU.CODGRUPOPROD)
		LEFT JOIN TPRMPS MPS ON (MPS.NUMPS = IPROC.NUMPS)
	WHERE
		IPA.IDIPROC = ?
	ORDER BY IPA.CODPRODPA, ORDER_NROLOTE, IPA.CONTROLEPA

) X
WHERE ROWNUM < 2

Params:
  1 = 12356

##ID_816## tempo: 2 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
entity: InstanciaAtividade
service-name: DatasetSP.loadRecords
uri: /mge/service.sbr
*/
SELECT TPRIPA.CODPRODPA AS CODPRODPA,TPRIPA.CONCLUIDO AS CONCLUIDO,TPRIPA.CONTROLEPA AS CONTROLEPA,TPRIPA.DTFAB AS DTFAB,TPRIPA.DTVAL AS DTVAL,TPRIPA.IDIPROC AS IDIPROC,TPRIPA.NROLOTE AS NROLOTE,TPRIPA.QTDPRODUZIR AS QTDPRODUZIR,TPRIPA.QTDPRODUZIR_ORIGINAL AS QTDPRODUZIR_ORIGINAL, ( SELECT REFERENCIA FROM TGFPRO PRO WHERE CODPROD = TPRIPA.CODPRODPA) AS REFERENCIA, ( 
	SELECT
		  TPRIPA.QTDPRODUZIR - NVL(SUM(NOTA.QTDNEG), 0) - (CASE
                                                       				WHEN NVL(SUM(NOTA.QTDNEG), 0) > 0 THEN NVL(MAX(APO_PERDA.QTDPERDA), 0)
                                                      				ELSE 0 
                                                      			  END) AS SALDO
	FROM
		TPRIPA IPA
	INNER JOIN TPRIPROC IPROC ON (IPA.IDIPROC = IPROC.IDIPROC)
	LEFT JOIN (
		SELECT IDIPROC, ITE.QTDNEG, ITE.CODPROD, ITE.CONTROLE 
		FROM TGFCAB CAB INNER JOIN TGFITE ITE ON (ITE.NUNOTA = CAB.NUNOTA)
						INNER JOIN TPRROPE ROPE ON (ROPE.NUNOTA = CAB.NUNOTA)
						INNER JOIN TPROEST OEST ON (OEST.IDEFX = ROPE.IDEFX AND OEST.SEQOPER = ROPE.SEQOPER)
		WHERE CAB.IDIPROC IS NOT NULL 
			AND OEST.TIPOITENS = 'PA'
			AND OEST.QUANDO = 'PA'
			AND CAB.TIPMOV = 'F'
	) NOTA ON (NOTA.IDIPROC = IPROC.IDIPROC AND NOTA.CODPROD = IPA.CODPRODPA AND (NVL(NOTA.CONTROLE, ' ') = ' ' OR NVL(NOTA.CONTROLE, ' ') = NVL(IPA.CONTROLEPA, ' ')))
	LEFT JOIN (
		SELECT  NVL(SUM(APA.QTDPERDA), 0) AS QTDPERDA , IATV.IDIPROC, APA.CODPRODPA, APA.CONTROLEPA
   		FROM TPRAPA APA
   		INNER JOIN TPRAPO APO ON(APO.NUAPO = APA.NUAPO)
   		INNER JOIN TPRIATV IATV ON(IATV.IDIATV = APO.IDIATV)
   		WHERE APO.SITUACAO = 'C'
   			AND APA.QTDPERDA > 0
		GROUP BY IATV.IDIPROC, APA.CODPRODPA, APA.CONTROLEPA
	) APO_PERDA ON (APO_PERDA.IDIPROC = IPROC.IDIPROC AND APO_PERDA.CODPRODPA = IPA.CODPRODPA AND (NVL(APO_PERDA.CONTROLEPA, ' ') = ' ' OR NVL(APO_PERDA.CONTROLEPA, ' ') = NVL(IPA.CONTROLEPA, ' ')))
	WHERE IPA.CODPRODPA = TPRIPA.CODPRODPA
		AND NVL(IPA.CONTROLEPA, ' ') = TPRIPA.CONTROLEPA
		AND IPROC.STATUSPROC IN ('A', 'R', 'P2', 'S', 'S2')
		AND IPROC.IDIPROC = TPRIPA.IDIPROC) AS SALDOOP FROM TPRIPA /*SQL_92_JOINED_TABLES*/   WHERE (TPRIPA.IDIPROC = ?) 
Params:
  1 = 12356

##ID_834## tempo: 1 (ms)
SELECT TPRIPA.CODPRODPA AS CODPRODPA,TPRIPA.CONCLUIDO AS CONCLUIDO,TPRIPA.CONTROLEPA AS CONTROLEPA,TPRIPA.DTFAB AS DTFAB,TPRIPA.DTVAL AS DTVAL,TPRIPA.IDIPROC AS IDIPROC,TPRIPA.NROLOTE AS NROLOTE,TPRIPA.QTDPRODUZIR AS QTDPRODUZIR,TPRIPA.QTDPRODUZIR_ORIGINAL AS QTDPRODUZIR_ORIGINAL, ( SELECT REFERENCIA FROM TGFPRO PRO WHERE CODPROD = TPRIPA.CODPRODPA) AS REFERENCIA, ( 
	SELECT
		  TPRIPA.QTDPRODUZIR - NVL(SUM(NOTA.QTDNEG), 0) - (CASE
                                                       				WHEN NVL(SUM(NOTA.QTDNEG), 0) > 0 THEN NVL(MAX(APO_PERDA.QTDPERDA), 0)
                                                      				ELSE 0 
                                                      			  END) AS SALDO
	FROM
		TPRIPA IPA
	INNER JOIN TPRIPROC IPROC ON (IPA.IDIPROC = IPROC.IDIPROC)
	LEFT JOIN (
		SELECT IDIPROC, ITE.QTDNEG, ITE.CODPROD, ITE.CONTROLE 
		FROM TGFCAB CAB INNER JOIN TGFITE ITE ON (ITE.NUNOTA = CAB.NUNOTA)
						INNER JOIN TPRROPE ROPE ON (ROPE.NUNOTA = CAB.NUNOTA)
						INNER JOIN TPROEST OEST ON (OEST.IDEFX = ROPE.IDEFX AND OEST.SEQOPER = ROPE.SEQOPER)
		WHERE CAB.IDIPROC IS NOT NULL 
			AND OEST.TIPOITENS = 'PA'
			AND OEST.QUANDO = 'PA'
			AND CAB.TIPMOV = 'F'
	) NOTA ON (NOTA.IDIPROC = IPROC.IDIPROC AND NOTA.CODPROD = IPA.CODPRODPA AND (NVL(NOTA.CONTROLE, ' ') = ' ' OR NVL(NOTA.CONTROLE, ' ') = NVL(IPA.CONTROLEPA, ' ')))
	LEFT JOIN (
		SELECT  NVL(SUM(APA.QTDPERDA), 0) AS QTDPERDA , IATV.IDIPROC, APA.CODPRODPA, APA.CONTROLEPA
   		FROM TPRAPA APA
   		INNER JOIN TPRAPO APO ON(APO.NUAPO = APA.NUAPO)
   		INNER JOIN TPRIATV IATV ON(IATV.IDIATV = APO.IDIATV)
   		WHERE APO.SITUACAO = 'C'
   			AND APA.QTDPERDA > 0
		GROUP BY IATV.IDIPROC, APA.CODPRODPA, APA.CONTROLEPA
	) APO_PERDA ON (APO_PERDA.IDIPROC = IPROC.IDIPROC AND APO_PERDA.CODPRODPA = IPA.CODPRODPA AND (NVL(APO_PERDA.CONTROLEPA, ' ') = ' ' OR NVL(APO_PERDA.CONTROLEPA, ' ') = NVL(IPA.CONTROLEPA, ' ')))
	WHERE IPA.CODPRODPA = TPRIPA.CODPRODPA
		AND NVL(IPA.CONTROLEPA, ' ') = TPRIPA.CONTROLEPA
		AND IPROC.STATUSPROC IN ('A', 'R', 'P2', 'S', 'S2')
		AND IPROC.IDIPROC = TPRIPA.IDIPROC) AS SALDOOP , Produto.DESCRPROD AS l0_DESCRPROD,Produto.COMPLDESC AS l0_COMPLDESC,Produto.CODVOL AS l0_CODVOL,Produto.DECQTD AS l0_DECQTD FROM TPRIPA  left join (SELECT CODVOL,COMPLDESC,DESCRPROD,DECQTD,CODPROD FROM TGFPRO) Produto  ON(TPRIPA.CODPRODPA = Produto.CODPROD)   WHERE (((TPRIPA.IDIPROC = ?)))

  1 = 12356.0

##ID_843## tempo: 1 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
entity: CabecalhoInstanciaProcesso
service-name: crud.find
uri: /mge/service.sbr
*/
SELECT TPRIPA.CODPRODPA AS CODPRODPA,TPRIPA.CONCLUIDO AS CONCLUIDO,TPRIPA.CONTROLEPA AS CONTROLEPA,TPRIPA.DTFAB AS DTFAB,TPRIPA.DTVAL AS DTVAL,TPRIPA.IDIPROC AS IDIPROC,TPRIPA.NROLOTE AS NROLOTE,TPRIPA.QTDPRODUZIR AS QTDPRODUZIR,TPRIPA.QTDPRODUZIR_ORIGINAL AS QTDPRODUZIR_ORIGINAL, ( SELECT REFERENCIA FROM TGFPRO PRO WHERE CODPROD = TPRIPA.CODPRODPA) AS REFERENCIA, ( 
	SELECT
		  TPRIPA.QTDPRODUZIR - NVL(SUM(NOTA.QTDNEG), 0) - (CASE
                                                       				WHEN NVL(SUM(NOTA.QTDNEG), 0) > 0 THEN NVL(MAX(APO_PERDA.QTDPERDA), 0)
                                                      				ELSE 0 
                                                      			  END) AS SALDO
	FROM
		TPRIPA IPA
	INNER JOIN TPRIPROC IPROC ON (IPA.IDIPROC = IPROC.IDIPROC)
	LEFT JOIN (
		SELECT IDIPROC, ITE.QTDNEG, ITE.CODPROD, ITE.CONTROLE 
		FROM TGFCAB CAB INNER JOIN TGFITE ITE ON (ITE.NUNOTA = CAB.NUNOTA)
						INNER JOIN TPRROPE ROPE ON (ROPE.NUNOTA = CAB.NUNOTA)
						INNER JOIN TPROEST OEST ON (OEST.IDEFX = ROPE.IDEFX AND OEST.SEQOPER = ROPE.SEQOPER)
		WHERE CAB.IDIPROC IS NOT NULL 
			AND OEST.TIPOITENS = 'PA'
			AND OEST.QUANDO = 'PA'
			AND CAB.TIPMOV = 'F'
	) NOTA ON (NOTA.IDIPROC = IPROC.IDIPROC AND NOTA.CODPROD = IPA.CODPRODPA AND (NVL(NOTA.CONTROLE, ' ') = ' ' OR NVL(NOTA.CONTROLE, ' ') = NVL(IPA.CONTROLEPA, ' ')))
	LEFT JOIN (
		SELECT  NVL(SUM(APA.QTDPERDA), 0) AS QTDPERDA , IATV.IDIPROC, APA.CODPRODPA, APA.CONTROLEPA
   		FROM TPRAPA APA
   		INNER JOIN TPRAPO APO ON(APO.NUAPO = APA.NUAPO)
   		INNER JOIN TPRIATV IATV ON(IATV.IDIATV = APO.IDIATV)
   		WHERE APO.SITUACAO = 'C'
   			AND APA.QTDPERDA > 0
		GROUP BY IATV.IDIPROC, APA.CODPRODPA, APA.CONTROLEPA
	) APO_PERDA ON (APO_PERDA.IDIPROC = IPROC.IDIPROC AND APO_PERDA.CODPRODPA = IPA.CODPRODPA AND (NVL(APO_PERDA.CONTROLEPA, ' ') = ' ' OR NVL(APO_PERDA.CONTROLEPA, ' ') = NVL(IPA.CONTROLEPA, ' ')))
	WHERE IPA.CODPRODPA = TPRIPA.CODPRODPA
		AND NVL(IPA.CONTROLEPA, ' ') = TPRIPA.CONTROLEPA
		AND IPROC.STATUSPROC IN ('A', 'R', 'P2', 'S', 'S2')

l0_CODPARC,CabecalhoNota.NUNOTA AS l0_NUNOTA,CabecalhoNota.NUMNOTA AS l0_NUMNOTA,CabecalhoNota.DTNEG AS l0_DTNEG,CabecalhoNota.CODEMP AS l0_CODEMP,CabecalhoNota.CODNAT AS NOMEFANTASIA,CODEMP FROM TSIEMP) Empresa2_1  ON(CabecalhoNota.CODEMP = Empresa2_1.CODEMP) left join (SELECT NOMEFANTASIA,CODEMP FROM TSIEMP) EmpresaNegociacao3_1  ON(CabecalhoNota.CODEMPNEGOC = ROPE.CODPRODPA = TPRROPE.CODPRODPA			AND ROPE.NUNOTA = TPRROPE.NUNOTA		GROUP BY ROPE.IDIATV, ROPE.IDEFX, ROPE.SEQOPER, ROPE.CODPRODPA, ROPE.NUNOTA))))

AS DHCAD,TPRLMP.ESTOQUETERCEIRO AS ESTOQUETERCEIRO,TPRLMP.FIXAQTDAPO AS FIXAQTDAPO,TPRLMP.GERAREQUISICAO AS GERAREQUISICAO,TPRLMP.IDEFX AS IDEFX,TPRLMP.LIBERADESVIO AS LIBERADESVIO,TPRLMP.PERCDESVIOINF AS PERCDESVIOINF,TPRLMP.PERCDESVIOSUP AS PERCDESVIOSUP,TPRLMP.PROPMPFIXA AS PROPMPFIXA,TPRLMP.QTDMISTURA AS QTDMISTURA,TPRLMP.SEQMP AS SEQMP,TPRLMP.TIPOCONTROLEMP AS TIPOCONTROLEMP,TPRLMP.TIPOQTD AS TIPOQTD,TPRLMP.TIPOUSOMP AS TIPOUSOMP,TPRLMP.VERIFICAEST AS VERIFICAEST,TPRLMP.VINCULOSERIEPA AS VINCULOSERIEPA, ( SELECT REFERENCIA FROM TGFPRO PRO WHERE CODPROD = TPRLMP.CODPRODMP) AS REFERENCIA , LocalBaixaMPProducao.DESCRLOCAL AS l0_DESCRLOCAL,LocalOrigemProducao.DESCRLOCAL AS l1_DESCRLOCAL,Produto.DESCRPROD AS l2_DESCRPROD,ProdutoMateriaPrima.DESCRPROD AS l3_DESCRPROD,ProdutoMateriaPrima.DECQTD AS l3_DECQTD,Usuario.NOMEUSU AS l4_NOMEUSU,Usuario2.NOMEUSU AS l5_NOMEUSU,Volume.DESCRVOL AS l6_DESCRVOL FROM TPRLMP  left join (SELECT DESCRLOCAL,CODLOCAL FROM TGFLOC) LocalBaixaMPProducao  ON(TPRLMP.CODLOCALBAIXA = LocalBaixaMPProducao.CODLOCAL) left join (SELECT DESCRLOCAL,CODLOCAL FROM TGFLOC) LocalOrigemProducao  ON(TPRLMP.CODLOCALORIG = LocalOrigemProducao.CODLOCAL) left join (SELECT DESCRPROD,CODPROD FROM TGFPRO) Produto  ON(TPRLMP.CODPRODPA = Produto.CODPROD) left join (SELECT DESCRPROD,DECQTD,CODPROD FROM TGFPRO) ProdutoMateriaPrima  ON(TPRLMP.CODPRODMP = ProdutoMateriaPrima.CODPROD) left join (SELECT CODUSU,NOMEUSU FROM TSIUSU) Usuario  ON(TPRLMP.CODUSUCAD = Usuario.CODUSU) left join (SELECT CODUSU,NOMEUSU FROM TSIUSU) Usuario2  ON(TPRLMP.CODUSUALT = Usuario2.CODUSU) left join (SELECT DESCRVOL,CODVOL FROM TGFVOL) Volume  ON(TPRLMP.CODVOL = Volume.CODVOL)   WHERE (((EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM TPRIPROC IPROC INNER JOIN TPREFX EFX ON (IPROC.IDPROC = EFX.IDPROC) WHERE EFX.IDEFX = TPRLMP.IDEFX AND IPROC.IDIPROC = ?) AND TPRLMP.IDEFX = ? AND TPRLMP.CODPRODPA = ? AND (NVL(TPRLMP.CONTROLEPA, ' ') = ' ' OR NVL(TPRLMP.CONTROLEPA, ' ') = ?))))  ORDER BY TPRLMP.SEQMP

VLRSUBSTUNITORIG,TGFITE.VLRTOT AS VLRTOT,TGFITE.VLRTOTMOE AS VLRTOTMOE,TGFITE.VLRTROCA AS VLRTROCA,TGFITE.VLRUNIT AS VLRUNIT,TGFITE.VLRUNITDOLAR AS VLRUNITDOLAR,TGFITE.VLRUNITLOC AS VLRUNITLOC,TGFITE.VLRUNITMOE AS VLRUNITMOE,TGFITE.VLRVENDAPROMO AS VLRVENDAPROMO, (

SELECT 

'Desc :'||ROUND(DESC_APLICADO*100,1)||'% - Desc Max: '||ROUND((DESC_COMER+DESC_ANTE)*100)||'% ('||ROUND(DESC_ANTE*100)||'% Desc antec '||ROUND(DESC_COMER*100)||'% Desc Comercial)' 

FROM VGF_DESCTAB_SATIS 
WHERE NUNOTA = TGFITE.NUNOTA 
AND SEQUENCIA = TGFITE.SEQUENCIA

/* ANTIGO VALOR 
SELECT 
DESCAPL||'- Desc. Máx: ' || TO_CHAR(DESC_COMER + DESC_ANT, 'FM990D00', 'NLS_NUMERIC_CHARACTERS='',.''') || '% ' || '('||DESC_ANT||'% Desc antec '|| ''||DESC_COMER||'% Desc Comercial)' 

FROM
(
SELECT 
'Desc: ' || TO_CHAR(ITE.PERCDESC, 'FM990D00', 'NLS_NUMERIC_CHARACTERS='',.''') || '% '  AS DESCAPL,

    (SELECT CASE WHEN AD_CLASCOMERCIAL = 'C' THEN 15 
      WHEN AD_CLASCOMERCIAL = 'R' THEN 35 
      WHEN AD_CLASCOMERCIAL IS NULL THEN 0 
    END  AS DESCONT
    FROM TGFPAR WHERE CODPARC = (SELECT CODPARC FROM TGFCAB WHERE NUNOTA = ITE.NUNOTA)) AS DESC_COMER,

    (SELECT NVL(SUM((NVL(M.PERCDESC,0) * NVL(V.PERC,0)) / 100 ),0)
       FROM AD_RATPROJ V 
       LEFT JOIN AD_DESCPERITE M ON (V.DTVENC >= M.DTINICIAL AND V.DTVENC <= M.DTFINAL)
       LEFT JOIN AD_DESCPERCAB CAB ON CAB.CODIGO = M.CODIGO
      WHERE V.NUNOTA = ITE.NUNOTA
      AND (SELECT MIN(DTVENC) + (MAX(DTVENC) - MIN(DTVENC)) / 2 
            FROM AD_RATPROJ FIN, TGFCAB CAB 
            WHERE CAB.NUNOTA = FIN.NUNOTA AND  FIN.NUNOTA = ITE.NUNOTA) BETWEEN CAB.DTINI AND CAB.DTFIN) AS DESC_ANT

FROM TGFITE ITE

WHERE ITE.NUNOTA = TGFITE.NUNOTA
AND ITE.SEQUENCIA = TGFITE.SEQUENCIA 
)

*/) AS AD_PERCDESCTAB, (
SELECT  NVL(ROUND( TGFITE.QTDNEG/VOA.QUANTIDADE,2),0) AS QTDPAL 
FROM TGFVOA VOA 
WHERE VOA.CODPROD = TGFITE.CODPROD
AND VOA.CODVOL='PL') AS AD_QTDPAL, ( 
CAST(
CAST(NVL(TGFITE.QTDNEG, 0) AS DECIMAL(38, 9)) - 
CAST(NVL(TGFITE.QTDENTREGUE, 0) AS DECIMAL(38, 9)) -
CAST(NVL(TGFITE.QTDCONFERIDA, 0) AS DECIMAL(38, 9))

AS FLOAT
)) AS AD_QTDPEND_PARCIAL, (
SELECT 
CASE WHEN (TOP.ATUALFIN=0)  AND TOP.CODTIPOPER <> 1112 THEN 0
WHEN TOP.ATUALFIN=-1 THEN SUM(ITE.QTDNEG * PRO.AD_QTDVOLLT)*-1
ELSE SUM(ITE.QTDNEG * PRO.AD_QTDVOLLT) END AS VOLUME
FROM TGFITE ITE, TGFPRO PRO, TGFTOP TOP, TGFCAB CAB
WHERE ITE.CODPROD=PRO.CODPROD
AND ITE.NUNOTA=TGFITE.NUNOTA
AND CAB.CODTIPOPER=TOP.CODTIPOPER
AND CAB.DHTIPOPER=TOP.DHALTER
AND CAB.NUNOTA=ITE.NUNOTA
AND ITE.SEQUENCIA=TGFITE.SEQUENCIA
GROUP BY TOP.ATUALFIN,  TOP.CODTIPOPER, TOP.ATUALEST) AS AD_QTDVLOLT, (
SELECT CASE WHEN (TOP.ATUALFIN=0 )  AND TOP.CODTIPOPER <> 1112 THEN 0
WHEN TOP.ATUALFIN=-1 THEN (ITE.VLRTOT-ITE.VLRDESC-ITE.VLRREPRED)*-1
ELSE (ITE.VLRTOT-ITE.VLRDESC-ITE.VLRREPRED) END AS VALORFIN
FROM TGFCAB CAB, TGFTOP TOP, TGFITE ITE
WHERE CAB.CODTIPOPER=TOP.CODTIPOPER
AND CAB.DHTIPOPER=TOP.DHALTER
AND CAB.NUNOTA=ITE.NUNOTA
AND ITE.NUNOTA=TGFITE.NUNOTA
AND ITE.SEQUENCIA=TGFITE.SEQUENCIA) AS AD_VLRFIN, (

SELECT 
PRECO_TAB
FROM VGF_DESCTAB_SATIS 
WHERE NUNOTA = TGFITE.NUNOTA 
AND SEQUENCIA = TGFITE.SEQUENCIA
 
/* DADOS ANTIGOS DE VALOR DE TABELA (AGORA BUSCA VALOR DE TABELA EM VIGOR )


    SELECT SNK_GET_PRECO(ITE.NUTAB,ITE.CODPROD,(SELECT NVL(MIN(DTVENC) + (MAX(DTVENC) - MIN(DTVENC)) / 2,SYSDATE) 
     FROM AD_RATPROJ FIN, TGFCAB CAB 
     WHERE CAB.NUNOTA = FIN.NUNOTA AND  FIN.NUNOTA = ITE.NUNOTA)) FROM TGFITE ITE WHERE ITE.NUNOTA = TGFITE.NUNOTA AND ITE.SEQUENCIA = TGFITE.SEQUENCIA  AND ITE.CODPROD = TGFITE.CODPROD

*/) AS AD_VLRUNITTAB, ( SELECT ITE.CODLOCALORIG FROM TGFITE ITE WHERE ITE.NUNOTA = TGFITE.NUNOTA AND ITE.SEQUENCIA < 0 AND ITE.SEQUENCIA = (TGFITE.SEQUENCIA * -1)) AS CODLOCALDEST, ( SELECT ITE.CONTROLE FROM TGFITE ITE WHERE ITE.NUNOTA = TGFITE.NUNOTA AND ITE.SEQUENCIA < 0 AND ITE.SEQUENCIA = (TGFITE.SEQUENCIA*-1)) AS CONTROLEDEST, ( CAST(CAST(NVL(TGFITE.QTDNEG, 0) AS DECIMAL(38, 9)) - CAST(NVL(TGFITE.QTDENTREGUE, 0) AS DECIMAL(38, 9)) AS FLOAT)) AS QTDPENDENTE, ( TGFITE.QTDNEG) AS QTDUNIDPAD, ( TGFITE.QTDNEG - TGFITE.QTDENTREGUE) AS RESERVADO, ( SELECT (CASE
           WHEN CAB.TIPMOV IN ('O', 'C', 'E')
              THEN (CASE WHEN NVL((SELECT LOGICO FROM TSIPAR WHERE CHAVE = 'DESCARRVLIQ'), 'N') = 'S' THEN (TGFITE.VLRUNIT * TGFITE.QTDNEG) ELSE TGFITE.VLRTOT END) - TGFITE.VLRDESC - TGFITE.VLRREPRED
           ELSE (CASE
                    WHEN NVL((SELECT INTEIRO
                                 FROM TSIPAR
                                WHERE CHAVE = 'TIPTABPRECOS'), 0) <> 9
                       THEN (CASE WHEN NVL((SELECT LOGICO FROM TSIPAR WHERE CHAVE = 'DESCARRVLIQ'), 'N') = 'S' THEN (TGFITE.VLRUNIT * TGFITE.QTDNEG) ELSE TGFITE.VLRTOT END) - TGFITE.VLRDESC - TGFITE.VLRREPRED
                    WHEN NVL((SELECT LOGICO
                            FROM TSIPAR
                           WHERE CHAVE = 'ADIMPVLRTOTLIQ'), 'S') <> 'S'
                       THEN (CASE WHEN NVL((SELECT LOGICO FROM TSIPAR WHERE CHAVE = 'DESCARRVLIQ'), 'N') = 'S' THEN (TGFITE.VLRUNIT * TGFITE.QTDNEG) ELSE TGFITE.VLRTOT END) - TGFITE.VLRDESC - TGFITE.VLRREPRED
                    ELSE   ((CASE WHEN NVL((SELECT LOGICO FROM TSIPAR WHERE CHAVE = 'DESCARRVLIQ'), 'N') = 'S' THEN (TGFITE.VLRUNIT * TGFITE.QTDNEG) ELSE TGFITE.VLRTOT END) - TGFITE.VLRDESC - TGFITE.VLRREPRED
                           )
                         + TGFITE.VLRSUBST
                         + ((CASE
                                WHEN TGFITE.VLRIPI > 0
                                AND NVL((SELECT SOMARIPI
                                            FROM TGFTOP TP
                                           WHERE TP.CODTIPOPER =
                                                                CAB.CODTIPOPER
                                             AND TP.DHALTER = CAB.DHTIPOPER),
                                         'N'
                                        ) <> 'N'
                                   THEN TGFITE.VLRIPI
                                ELSE 0
                             END
                            )
                           )
                 END
                )
        END
       )
  FROM TGFCAB CAB
 WHERE CAB.NUNOTA = TGFITE.NUNOTA) AS VLRTOTLIQ, ( SELECT (CASE WHEN CAB.TIPMOV IN('O','C','E') THEN TGFITE.VLRTOTMOE - TGFITE.VLRDESCMOE - TGFITE.VLRREPRED ELSE (CASE WHEN NVL((SELECT INTEIRO FROM TSIPAR WHERE CHAVE = 'TIPTABPRECO'),0) <> 9 THEN TGFITE.VLRTOTMOE - TGFITE.VLRDESCMOE - TGFITE.VLRREPRED ELSE (TGFITE.VLRTOTMOE - TGFITE.VLRDESCMOE - TGFITE.VLRREPRED) + TGFITE.VLRSUBST + ((CASE WHEN TGFITE.VLRIPI > 0 AND NVL((SELECT SOMARIPI FROM TGFTOP TP WHERE TP.CODTIPOPER = CAB.CODTIPOPER AND TP.DHALTER = CAB.DHTIPOPER),'N') <> 'N' THEN TGFITE.VLRIPI ELSE 0 END)) END) END) FROM TGFCAB CAB WHERE CAB.NUNOTA = TGFITE.NUNOTA) AS VLRTOTLIQMOE, ( TGFITE.VLRUNIT) AS VLRUNIDPAD, ( SELECT (CASE WHEN TGFITE.QTDNEG = 0 THEN 0 ELSE (CASE WHEN CAB.TIPMOV IN('O','C','E') THEN (CASE WHEN NVL((SELECT LOGICO FROM TSIPAR WHERE CHAVE = 'DESCARRVLIQ'), 'N') = 'S' THEN (TGFITE.VLRUNIT * TGFITE.QTDNEG) ELSE TGFITE.VLRTOT END) - TGFITE.VLRDESC - TGFITE.VLRREPRED ELSE (CASE WHEN NVL((SELECT INTEIRO FROM TSIPAR WHERE CHAVE = 'TIPTABPRECO'),0) <> 9 THEN (CASE WHEN NVL((SELECT LOGICO FROM TSIPAR WHERE CHAVE = 'DESCARRVLIQ'), 'N') = 'S' THEN (TGFITE.VLRUNIT * TGFITE.QTDNEG) ELSE TGFITE.VLRTOT END) - TGFITE.VLRDESC - TGFITE.VLRREPRED ELSE ((CASE WHEN NVL((SELECT LOGICO FROM TSIPAR WHERE CHAVE = 'DESCARRVLIQ'), 'N') = 'S' THEN (TGFITE.VLRUNIT * TGFITE.QTDNEG) ELSE TGFITE.VLRTOT END) - TGFITE.VLRDESC - TGFITE.VLRREPRED) + TGFITE.VLRSUBST + ((CASE WHEN TGFITE.VLRIPI > 0 AND NVL((SELECT SOMARIPI FROM TGFTOP TP WHERE TP.CODTIPOPER = CAB.CODTIPOPER AND TP.DHALTER = CAB.DHTIPOPER),'N') <> 'N' THEN TGFITE.VLRIPI ELSE 0 END)) END) END) / TGFITE.QTDNEG END) FROM TGFCAB CAB WHERE CAB.NUNOTA = TGFITE.NUNOTA) AS VLRUNITLIQ, ( SELECT (CASE WHEN TGFITE.QTDNEG = 0 THEN 0 ELSE (CASE WHEN CAB.TIPMOV IN('O','C','E') THEN TGFITE.VLRTOTMOE - TGFITE.VLRDESCMOE - TGFITE.VLRREPRED ELSE (CASE WHEN NVL((SELECT INTEIRO FROM TSIPAR WHERE CHAVE = 'TIPTABPRECO'),0) <> 9 THEN TGFITE.VLRTOTMOE - TGFITE.VLRDESCMOE - TGFITE.VLRREPRED ELSE (TGFITE.VLRTOTMOE - TGFITE.VLRDESCMOE - TGFITE.VLRREPRED) + TGFITE.VLRSUBST + ((CASE WHEN TGFITE.VLRIPI > 0 AND NVL((SELECT SOMARIPI FROM TGFTOP TP WHERE TP.CODTIPOPER = CAB.CODTIPOPER AND TP.DHALTER = CAB.DHTIPOPER),'N') <> 'N' THEN TGFITE.VLRIPI ELSE 0 END)) END) END) / TGFITE.QTDNEG END) FROM TGFCAB CAB WHERE CAB.NUNOTA = TGFITE.NUNOTA) AS VLRUNITLIQMOE , LocalFinanceiro.DESCRLOCAL AS l0_DESCRLOCAL,Produto.DESCRPROD AS l1_DESCRPROD,Produto.DECVLR AS l1_DECVLR,Produto.DECQTD AS l1_DECQTD,Volume.DESCRVOL AS l2_DESCRVOL FROM TGFITE  left join (SELECT DESCRLOCAL,CODLOCAL FROM TGFLOC) LocalFinanceiro  ON(TGFITE.CODLOCALORIG = LocalFinanceiro.CODLOCAL) left join (SELECT DESCRPROD,DECQTD,CODPROD,DECVLR FROM TGFPRO) Produto  ON(TGFITE.CODPROD = Produto.CODPROD) left join (SELECT DESCRVOL,CODVOL FROM TGFVOL) Volume  ON(TGFITE.CODVOL = Volume.CODVOL)   WHERE (((TGFITE.SEQUENCIA > 0AND TGFITE.NUNOTA = 127686)))

##ID_974## tempo: 1 (ms)
/* Runtime-info

 SELECT ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.CODINSTPRINC, REG.TIPO FROM TGFITR ITR   INNER JOIN TGFREG REG ON (REG.CODREGRA = ITR.CODREGRA)   INNER JOIN TGFCER CER ON (CER.CODREGRA = REG.CODREGRA) WHERE   CER.TIPO = 'U'    AND CER.ATIVO = 'S'    AND ITR.ATIVO = 'S'    AND CER.CHAVE = ?    AND TRANSLATE(UPPER(REG.INSTPRINC),'ÁÉÍÓÚÃÕÂÊÎÔÛÀÈÌÒÙÇ','AEIOUAOAEIOUAEIOUC') = ?   AND CER.FILTRAR = 'S'    AND (REG.INSTSEC IS NULL OR REG.INSTSEC = '')  ORDER BY ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.SEQUENCIA

##ID_232## tempo: 2 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
service-name: OperacaoProducaoSP.criarApontamento
uri: /mgeprod/service.sbr
*/
SELECT TPRIPA.CODPRODPA AS CODPRODPA,TPRIPA.CONCLUIDO AS CONCLUIDO,TPRIPA.CONTROLEPA AS CONTROLEPA,TPRIPA.DTFAB AS DTFAB,TPRIPA.DTVAL AS DTVAL,TPRIPA.IDIPROC AS IDIPROC,TPRIPA.NROLOTE AS NROLOTE,TPRIPA.QTDPRODUZIR AS QTDPRODUZIR,TPRIPA.QTDPRODUZIR_ORIGINAL AS QTDPRODUZIR_ORIGINAL, ( SELECT REFERENCIA FROM TGFPRO PRO WHERE CODPROD = TPRIPA.CODPRODPA) AS REFERENCIA, ( 
	SELECT
		  TPRIPA.QTDPRODUZIR - NVL(SUM(NOTA.QTDNEG), 0) - (CASE
                                                       				WHEN NVL(SUM(NOTA.QTDNEG), 0) > 0 THEN NVL(MAX(APO_PERDA.QTDPERDA), 0)
                                                      				ELSE 0 
                                                      			  END) AS SALDO
	FROM
		TPRIPA IPA
	INNER JOIN TPRIPROC IPROC ON (IPA.IDIPROC = IPROC.IDIPROC)
	LEFT JOIN (
		SELECT IDIPROC, ITE.QTDNEG, ITE.CODPROD, ITE.CONTROLE 
		FROM TGFCAB CAB INNER JOIN TGFITE ITE ON (ITE.NUNOTA = CAB.NUNOTA)
						INNER JOIN TPRROPE ROPE ON (ROPE.NUNOTA = CAB.NUNOTA)
						INNER JOIN TPROEST OEST ON (OEST.IDEFX = ROPE.IDEFX AND OEST.SEQOPER = ROPE.SEQOPER)
		WHERE CAB.IDIPROC IS NOT NULL 
			AND OEST.TIPOITENS = 'PA'
			AND OEST.QUANDO = 'PA'
			AND CAB.TIPMOV = 'F'
	) NOTA ON (NOTA.IDIPROC = IPROC.IDIPROC AND NOTA.CODPROD = IPA.CODPRODPA AND (NVL(NOTA.CONTROLE, ' ') = ' ' OR NVL(NOTA.CONTROLE, ' ') = NVL(IPA.CONTROLEPA, ' ')))
	LEFT JOIN (
		SELECT  NVL(SUM(APA.QTDPERDA), 0) AS QTDPERDA , IATV.IDIPROC, APA.CODPRODPA, APA.CONTROLEPA
   		FROM TPRAPA APA
   		INNER JOIN TPRAPO APO ON(APO.NUAPO = APA.NUAPO)
   		INNER JOIN TPRIATV IATV ON(IATV.IDIATV = APO.IDIATV)
   		WHERE APO.SITUACAO = 'C'
   			AND APA.QTDPERDA > 0
		GROUP BY IATV.IDIPROC, APA.CODPRODPA, APA.CONTROLEPA
	) APO_PERDA ON (APO_PERDA.IDIPROC = IPROC.IDIPROC AND APO_PERDA.CODPRODPA = IPA.CODPRODPA AND (NVL(APO_PERDA.CONTROLEPA, ' ') = ' ' OR NVL(APO_PERDA.CONTROLEPA, ' ') = NVL(IPA.CONTROLEPA, ' ')))
	WHERE IPA.CODPRODPA = TPRIPA.CODPRODPA
		AND NVL(IPA.CONTROLEPA, ' ') = TPRIPA.CONTROLEPA
		AND IPROC.STATUSPROC IN ('A', 'R', 'P2', 'S', 'S2')
		AND IPROC.IDIPROC = TPRIPA.IDIPROC) AS SALDOOP FROM TPRIPA /*SQL_92_JOINED_TABLES*/   WHERE (TPRIPA.IDIPROC = ?) 
Params:
  1 = 12356

##ID_233## tempo: 2 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
service-name: OperacaoProducaoSP.criarApontamento

SELECT TSIPAR.ABA AS ABA,TSIPAR.CHAVE AS CHAVE,TSIPAR.CLASSE AS CLASSE,TSIPAR.CODUSU AS CODUSU,TSIPAR.DATA AS DATA,TSIPAR.DESCRICAO AS DESCRICAO,TSIPAR.INTEIRO AS INTEIRO,TSIPAR.LOGICO AS LOGICO,TSIPAR.MODULO AS MODULO,TSIPAR.NUMDEC AS NUMDEC,TSIPAR.TEXTO AS TEXTO,TSIPAR.TIPO AS TIPO FROM TSIPAR /*SQL_92_JOINED_TABLES*/  WHERE (TSIPAR.CHAVE = ? ##ID_249## tempo: 2 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
service-name: OperacaoProducaoSP.criarApontamento
uri: /mgeprod/service.sbr
*/
SELECT 
X.CODPRODMP,
X.CONTROLEMP,
SUM(X.QTDMISTURA) AS QTDMISTURA,
X.PROPMPFIXA,
X.CODVOL
 ,X.CODLOCALORIG,
X.TIPOUSOMP,
X.FIXAQTDAPO,
X.TIPOQTD,
X.VINCULOSERIEPA 
FROM(
	SELECT
	LMP.CODPRODMP,
	(CASE 
	WHEN LMP.TIPOCONTROLEMP = 'L' 
		THEN LMP.CONTROLEMP
	WHEN LMP.TIPOCONTROLEMP = 'H'    
		THEN ?
	ELSE 
		' '	
	END
	) AS CONTROLEMP,
	(CASE WHEN LMP.TIPOQTD = 'V' THEN LMP.QTDMISTURA * ? ELSE LMP.QTDMISTURA END) AS QTDMISTURA,
	LMP.PROPMPFIXA,
	NVL(LMP.CODVOL, PRO.CODVOL) AS CODVOL
	 ,LMP.CODLOCALORIG, 
	LMP.TIPOUSOMP,
	LMP.FIXAQTDAPO,
	LMP.TIPOQTD,
	NVL(LMP.VINCULOSERIEPA,'N') AS VINCULOSERIEPA 
	FROM TPRLMP LMP
	INNER JOIN TPREFX EFX ON(EFX.IDEFX = LMP.IDEFX)
	INNER JOIN TPRATV ATV ON(ATV.IDEFX = LMP.IDEFX)
	INNER JOIN TGFPRO PRO ON (PRO.CODPROD = LMP.CODPRODMP )
	WHERE
	EFX.IDPROC = ?
	AND ((? = 0 AND ATV.LISTAMPPADRAO = 'S') OR (? > 0 AND ATV.IDEFX = ?))
	AND (? = 'T' OR LMP.GERAREQUISICAO = ?)
	AND LMP.CODPRODPA = ?
	 AND (LMP.TIPOUSOMP IN ('N'))  
	--TIPO_MATERIAL AND 
	AND (
		(NVL(LMP.CONTROLEPA,' ') <> ' ' AND NVL(LMP.CONTROLEPA,' ') = ?)
		OR (
		NVL(LMP.CONTROLEPA, ' ') = ' '
		AND NOT EXISTS(
			SELECT 1 
			FROM TPRLMP LMP2 
			WHERE
			LMP2.IDEFX = LMP.IDEFX
			AND LMP2.CODPRODPA = LMP.CODPRODPA
			AND NVL(LMP2.CONTROLEPA,' ') = ?
			AND LMP2.CODPRODMP = LMP.CODPRODMP
			AND LMP2.CONTROLEMP = LMP.CONTROLEMP
			AND LMP2.SEQMP <> LMP.SEQMP
			)
		)
	)
) X
GROUP BY X.CODPRODMP,X.PROPMPFIXA,X.CONTROLEMP,X.CODVOL ,X.CODLOCALORIG,X.TIPOUSOMP,X.FIXAQTDAPO,X.TIPOQTD,X.VINCULOSERIEPA 
Params:
  1 =  
  2 = 160
  3 = 30
  4 = 0
  5 = 0
  6 = 0
  7 = T
  8 = T
  9 = 4
  10 =  
  11 =  
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
##ID_250## tempo: 0 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5

 SELECT ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.CODINSTPRINC, REG.TIPO FROM TGFITR ITR   INNER JOIN TGFREG REG ON (REG.CODREGRA = ITR.CODREGRA)   INNER JOIN TGFCER CER ON (CER.CODREGRA = REG.CODREGRA) WHERE   CER.TIPO = 'U'    AND CER.ATIVO = 'S'    AND ITR.ATIVO = 'S'    AND CER.CHAVE = ?    AND TRANSLATE(UPPER(REG.INSTPRINC),'\C1\C9\CD\D3\DA\C3\D5\C2\CA\CE\D4\DB\C0\C8\CC\D2\D9\C7','AEIOUAOAEIOUAEIOUC') = ?   AND CER.FILTRAR = 'S'    AND (REG.INSTSEC IS NULL OR REG.INSTSEC = '')  ORDER BY ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.SEQUENCIA

##ID_254## tempo: 1 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
service-name: OperacaoProducaoSP.criarApontamento
uri: /mgeprod/service.sbr
*/
 SELECT ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.CODINSTPRINC, REG.TIPO FROM TGFITR ITR   INNER JOIN TGFREG REG ON (REG.CODREGRA = ITR.CODREGRA)   INNER JOIN TGFCER CER ON (CER.CODREGRA = REG.CODREGRA) WHERE   CER.TIPO = 'U'    AND CER.ATIVO = 'S'    AND ITR.ATIVO = 'S'    AND CER.CHAVE = ?    AND TRANSLATE(UPPER(REG.INSTPRINC),'\C1\C9\CD\D3\DA\C3\D5\C2\CA\CE\D4\DB\C0\C8\CC\D2\D9\C7','AEIOUAOAEIOUAEIOUC') = ?   AND CER.FILTRAR = 'S'    AND (REG.INSTSEC IS NULL OR REG.INSTSEC = '')  ORDER BY ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.SEQUENCIA
Params:
  1 = 0
  2 = PRODUTO
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
##ID_255## tempo: 1 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
service-name: OperacaoProducaoSP.criarApontamento
uri: /mgeprod/service.sbr
*/
 SELECT ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.CODINSTPRINC, REG.TIPO FROM TGFITR ITR   INNER JOIN TGFREG REG ON (REG.CODREGRA = ITR.CODREGRA)   INNER JOIN TGFCER CER ON (CER.CODREGRA = REG.CODREGRA) WHERE   CER.TIPO = 'U'    AND CER.ATIVO = 'S'    AND ITR.ATIVO = 'S'    AND CER.CHAVE = ?    AND TRANSLATE(UPPER(REG.INSTPRINC),'\C1\C9\CD\D3\DA\C3\D5\C2\CA\CE\D4\DB\C0\C8\CC\D2\D9\C7','AEIOUAOAEIOUAEIOUC') = ?   AND CER.FILTRAR = 'S'    AND (REG.INSTSEC IS NULL OR REG.INSTSEC = '')  ORDER BY ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.SEQUENCIA
Params:
  1 = 0
  2 = GRUPO DE PRODUTO

##ID_258## tempo: 1 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
service-name: OperacaoProducaoSP.criarApontamento
uri: /mgeprod/service.sbr
*/
 SELECT ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.CODINSTPRINC, REG.TIPO FROM TGFITR ITR   INNER JOIN TGFREG REG ON (REG.CODREGRA = ITR.CODREGRA)   INNER JOIN TGFCER CER ON (CER.CODREGRA = REG.CODREGRA) WHERE   CER.TIPO = 'U'    AND CER.ATIVO = 'S'    AND ITR.ATIVO = 'S'    AND CER.CHAVE = ?    AND TRANSLATE(UPPER(REG.INSTPRINC),'\C1\C9\CD\D3\DA\C3\D5\C2\CA\CE\D4\DB\C0\C8\CC\D2\D9\C7','AEIOUAOAEIOUAEIOUC') = ?   AND CER.FILTRAR = 'S'    AND (REG.INSTSEC IS NULL OR REG.INSTSEC = '')  ORDER BY ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.SEQUENCIA
Params:
  1 = 0
  2 = PRODUTO
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
##ID_259## tempo: 1 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
service-name: OperacaoProducaoSP.criarApontamento
uri: /mgeprod/service.sbr
*/
 SELECT ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.CODINSTPRINC, REG.TIPO FROM TGFITR ITR   INNER JOIN TGFREG REG ON (REG.CODREGRA = ITR.CODREGRA)   INNER JOIN TGFCER CER ON (CER.CODREGRA = REG.CODREGRA) WHERE   CER.TIPO = 'U'    AND CER.ATIVO = 'S'    AND ITR.ATIVO = 'S'    AND CER.CHAVE = ?    AND TRANSLATE(UPPER(REG.INSTPRINC),'\C1\C9\CD\D3\DA\C3\D5\C2\CA\CE\D4\DB\C0\C8\CC\D2\D9\C7','AEIOUAOAEIOUAEIOUC') = ?   AND CER.FILTRAR = 'S'    AND (REG.INSTSEC IS NULL OR REG.INSTSEC = '')  ORDER BY ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.SEQUENCIA
Params:
  1 = 0
  2 = GRUPO DE PRODUTO

##ID_262## tempo: 1 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
service-name: OperacaoProducaoSP.criarApontamento
uri: /mgeprod/service.sbr
*/
 SELECT ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.CODINSTPRINC, REG.TIPO FROM TGFITR ITR   INNER JOIN TGFREG REG ON (REG.CODREGRA = ITR.CODREGRA)   INNER JOIN TGFCER CER ON (CER.CODREGRA = REG.CODREGRA) WHERE   CER.TIPO = 'U'    AND CER.ATIVO = 'S'    AND ITR.ATIVO = 'S'    AND CER.CHAVE = ?    AND TRANSLATE(UPPER(REG.INSTPRINC),'\C1\C9\CD\D3\DA\C3\D5\C2\CA\CE\D4\DB\C0\C8\CC\D2\D9\C7','AEIOUAOAEIOUAEIOUC') = ?   AND CER.FILTRAR = 'S'    AND (REG.INSTSEC IS NULL OR REG.INSTSEC = '')  ORDER BY ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.SEQUENCIA
Params:
  1 = 0
  2 = PRODUTO
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
##ID_263## tempo: 2 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
service-name: OperacaoProducaoSP.criarApontamento
uri: /mgeprod/service.sbr
*/
 SELECT ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.CODINSTPRINC, REG.TIPO FROM TGFITR ITR   INNER JOIN TGFREG REG ON (REG.CODREGRA = ITR.CODREGRA)   INNER JOIN TGFCER CER ON (CER.CODREGRA = REG.CODREGRA) WHERE   CER.TIPO = 'U'    AND CER.ATIVO = 'S'    AND ITR.ATIVO = 'S'    AND CER.CHAVE = ?    AND TRANSLATE(UPPER(REG.INSTPRINC),'\C1\C9\CD\D3\DA\C3\D5\C2\CA\CE\D4\DB\C0\C8\CC\D2\D9\C7','AEIOUAOAEIOUAEIOUC') = ?   AND CER.FILTRAR = 'S'    AND (REG.INSTSEC IS NULL OR REG.INSTSEC = '')  ORDER BY ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.SEQUENCIA
Params:
  1 = 0
  2 = GRUPO DE PRODUTO

##ID_266## tempo: 1 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
service-name: OperacaoProducaoSP.criarApontamento
uri: /mgeprod/service.sbr
*/
 SELECT ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.CODINSTPRINC, REG.TIPO FROM TGFITR ITR   INNER JOIN TGFREG REG ON (REG.CODREGRA = ITR.CODREGRA)   INNER JOIN TGFCER CER ON (CER.CODREGRA = REG.CODREGRA) WHERE   CER.TIPO = 'U'    AND CER.ATIVO = 'S'    AND ITR.ATIVO = 'S'    AND CER.CHAVE = ?    AND TRANSLATE(UPPER(REG.INSTPRINC),'\C1\C9\CD\D3\DA\C3\D5\C2\CA\CE\D4\DB\C0\C8\CC\D2\D9\C7','AEIOUAOAEIOUAEIOUC') = ?   AND CER.FILTRAR = 'S'    AND (REG.INSTSEC IS NULL OR REG.INSTSEC = '')  ORDER BY ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.SEQUENCIA
Params:
  1 = 0
  2 = PRODUTO
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
##ID_267## tempo: 1 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
service-name: OperacaoProducaoSP.criarApontamento
uri: /mgeprod/service.sbr
*/
 SELECT ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.CODINSTPRINC, REG.TIPO FROM TGFITR ITR   INNER JOIN TGFREG REG ON (REG.CODREGRA = ITR.CODREGRA)   INNER JOIN TGFCER CER ON (CER.CODREGRA = REG.CODREGRA) WHERE   CER.TIPO = 'U'    AND CER.ATIVO = 'S'    AND ITR.ATIVO = 'S'    AND CER.CHAVE = ?    AND TRANSLATE(UPPER(REG.INSTPRINC),'\C1\C9\CD\D3\DA\C3\D5\C2\CA\CE\D4\DB\C0\C8\CC\D2\D9\C7','AEIOUAOAEIOUAEIOUC') = ?   AND CER.FILTRAR = 'S'    AND (REG.INSTSEC IS NULL OR REG.INSTSEC = '')  ORDER BY ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.SEQUENCIA
Params:
  1 = 0
  2 = GRUPO DE PRODUTO
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

##ID_270## tempo: 1 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
service-name: OperacaoProducaoSP.criarApontamento
uri: /mgeprod/service.sbr
*/
 SELECT ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.CODINSTPRINC, REG.TIPO FROM TGFITR ITR   INNER JOIN TGFREG REG ON (REG.CODREGRA = ITR.CODREGRA)   INNER JOIN TGFCER CER ON (CER.CODREGRA = REG.CODREGRA) WHERE   CER.TIPO = 'U'    AND CER.ATIVO = 'S'    AND ITR.ATIVO = 'S'    AND CER.CHAVE = ?    AND TRANSLATE(UPPER(REG.INSTPRINC),'\C1\C9\CD\D3\DA\C3\D5\C2\CA\CE\D4\DB\C0\C8\CC\D2\D9\C7','AEIOUAOAEIOUAEIOUC') = ?   AND CER.FILTRAR = 'S'    AND (REG.INSTSEC IS NULL OR REG.INSTSEC = '')  ORDER BY ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.SEQUENCIA
Params:
  1 = 0
  2 = PRODUTO
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
##ID_271## tempo: 1 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
service-name: OperacaoProducaoSP.criarApontamento
uri: /mgeprod/service.sbr
*/
 SELECT ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.CODINSTPRINC, REG.TIPO FROM TGFITR ITR   INNER JOIN TGFREG REG ON (REG.CODREGRA = ITR.CODREGRA)   INNER JOIN TGFCER CER ON (CER.CODREGRA = REG.CODREGRA) WHERE   CER.TIPO = 'U'    AND CER.ATIVO = 'S'    AND ITR.ATIVO = 'S'    AND CER.CHAVE = ?    AND TRANSLATE(UPPER(REG.INSTPRINC),'\C1\C9\CD\D3\DA\C3\D5\C2\CA\CE\D4\DB\C0\C8\CC\D2\D9\C7','AEIOUAOAEIOUAEIOUC') = ?   AND CER.FILTRAR = 'S'    AND (REG.INSTSEC IS NULL OR REG.INSTSEC = '')  ORDER BY ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.SEQUENCIA
Params:
  1 = 0

##ID_274## tempo: 1 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
service-name: OperacaoProducaoSP.criarApontamento
uri: /mgeprod/service.sbr
*/
 SELECT ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.CODINSTPRINC, REG.TIPO FROM TGFITR ITR   INNER JOIN TGFREG REG ON (REG.CODREGRA = ITR.CODREGRA)   INNER JOIN TGFCER CER ON (CER.CODREGRA = REG.CODREGRA) WHERE   CER.TIPO = 'U'    AND CER.ATIVO = 'S'    AND ITR.ATIVO = 'S'    AND CER.CHAVE = ?    AND TRANSLATE(UPPER(REG.INSTPRINC),'\C1\C9\CD\D3\DA\C3\D5\C2\CA\CE\D4\DB\C0\C8\CC\D2\D9\C7','AEIOUAOAEIOUAEIOUC') = ?   AND CER.FILTRAR = 'S'    AND (REG.INSTSEC IS NULL OR REG.INSTSEC = '')  ORDER BY ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.SEQUENCIA
Params:
  1 = 0
  2 = PRODUTO
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
##ID_275## tempo: 0 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
service-name: OperacaoProducaoSP.criarApontamento
uri: /mgeprod/service.sbr
*/
 SELECT ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.CODINSTPRINC, REG.TIPO FROM TGFITR ITR   INNER JOIN TGFREG REG ON (REG.CODREGRA = ITR.CODREGRA)   INNER JOIN TGFCER CER ON (CER.CODREGRA = REG.CODREGRA) WHERE   CER.TIPO = 'U'    AND CER.ATIVO = 'S'    AND ITR.ATIVO = 'S'    AND CER.CHAVE = ?    AND TRANSLATE(UPPER(REG.INSTPRINC),'\C1\C9\CD\D3\DA\C3\D5\C2\CA\CE\D4\DB\C0\C8\CC\D2\D9\C7','AEIOUAOAEIOUAEIOUC') = ?   AND CER.FILTRAR = 'S'    AND (REG.INSTSEC IS NULL OR REG.INSTSEC = '')  ORDER BY ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.SEQUENCIA
Params:
  1 = 0
  2 = GRUPO DE PRODUTO

##ID_278## tempo: 2 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
service-name: OperacaoProducaoSP.criarApontamento
uri: /mgeprod/service.sbr
*/
SELECT DISTINCT X.CODPRODMPALT, 
                X.QTD_SUB, 
                X.QTDMISTURA, 
                X.QTD, 
                X.CONJUNTO, 
                X.CONTROLEMPALT, 
                X.CODVOL,
                X.ORDEM,
                X.CODLOCALORIG,
                X.CODLOCALBAIXA
FROM   (SELECT DISTINCT MPA.CODPRODMPALT, 
                        IMPA.QTDMISTURA / MPA.QTDMISTURA AS QTD_SUB, 
                        IMPA.QTDMISTURA, 
                        MPA.QTDMISTURA AS QTD, 
                        MPA.CONJUNTO, 
                        MPA.CONTROLEMPALT, 
                        MPA.CODVOL, 
                        IMPA.ORDEM ,
                        MPA.CODLOCALORIG,
                        MPA.CODLOCALBAIXA
        FROM   TPRMPA MPA 
               INNER JOIN TPRIMPA IMPA 
                       ON ( MPA.CODPRODPA = IMPA.CODPRODPA

##ID_287## tempo: 131 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
service-name: OperacaoProducaoSP.criarApontamento
uri: /mgeprod/service.sbr
*/
 SELECT TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL AS DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX AS IDEFX,  	   SUM(CASE WHEN (TPRIATV.IDEFX = ? OR ? = 0) THEN TGFITE.QTDNEG ELSE 0 END) AS QTDNEG  	FROM TGFITE INNER JOIN TGFCAB ON (TGFITE.NUNOTA = TGFCAB.NUNOTA) 					INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT CODPROD, CONTROLE, DTVAL FROM TGFEST) TGFEST ON (TGFEST.CODPROD = TGFITE.CODPROD AND TGFEST.CONTROLE = TGFITE.CONTROLE) 					INNER JOIN TPRROPE ON TGFCAB.NUNOTA = TPRROPE.NUNOTA 					INNER JOIN TPRIATV ON (TPRIATV.IDIATV = TPRROPE.IDIATV AND TGFCAB.IDIPROC = TPRIATV.IDIPROC) 	WHERE TGFCAB.IDIPROC = ?  	AND TGFITE.CODPROD = ?   	AND TGFITE.SEQUENCIA > 0  	AND TGFCAB.TIPMOV <> 'F'  GROUP BY TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX  UNION  SELECT TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL AS DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX AS IDEFX,  	   SUM(CASE WHEN TPRIATV.IDEFX != ? THEN TGFITE.QTDNEG ELSE 0 END) AS QTDNEG  	FROM TGFITE INNER JOIN TGFCAB ON (TGFITE.NUNOTA = TGFCAB.NUNOTA) 					INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT CODPROD, CONTROLE, DTVAL FROM TGFEST) TGFEST ON (TGFEST.CODPROD = TGFITE.CODPROD AND TGFEST.CONTROLE = TGFITE.CONTROLE) 					INNER JOIN TPRROPE ON TGFCAB.NUNOTA = TPRROPE.NUNOTA 					INNER JOIN TPRIATV ON (TPRIATV.IDIATV = TPRROPE.IDIATV AND TGFCAB.IDIPROC = TPRIATV.IDIPROC) 	WHERE TGFCAB.IDIPROC = ?  	AND TGFITE.CODPROD = ?   	AND TGFITE.SEQUENCIA > 0  	AND TGFCAB.TIPMOV <> 'F'  GROUP BY TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX  ORDER BY IDEFX DESC, DTVAL ASC 
Params:
  1 = 244
  2 = 244
  3 = 12356
  4 = 6
  5 = 244
  6 = 12356
  7 = 6

AND TPRAMP.CODPRODMP = ?  GROUP BY TPRAMP.CODPRODMP, TPRAMP.CONTROLEMP, TPRAMP.CODVOL, TGFPRO.CODVOL

##ID_290## tempo: 2 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
service-name: OperacaoProducaoSP.criarApontamento
uri: /mgeprod/service.sbr
*/
SELECT
	IPROC.IDIPROC,
	IATV.IDIATV,
	APA.CODPRODPA,
	APA.CONTROLEPA,
	PROMP.USALOCAL,
	PROPA.TIPCONTEST AS TIPCONTESTPA,
	PROMP.TIPCONTEST AS TIPCONTESTMP,
	OEST.CODLOCALBAIXAMP 
FROM
	TPRIPROC IPROC
INNER JOIN TPRIATV IATV ON
	(IPROC.IDIPROC = IATV.IDIPROC)
INNER JOIN TPRAPO APO ON
	(APO.IDIATV = IATV.IDIATV)
INNER JOIN TPRAPA APA ON
	(APA.NUAPO = APO.NUAPO)
INNER JOIN TGFPRO PROMP ON
	(PROMP.CODPROD = ?)
INNER JOIN TGFPRO PROPA ON
	(PROPA.CODPROD = APA.CODPRODPA)
LEFT JOIN TPROEST OEST ON
	(OEST.IDEFX  IN (SELECT IDEFX FROM TPRATV WHERE IDPROC = IPROC.IDPROC))
WHERE

 SELECT TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL AS DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX AS IDEFX,  	   SUM(CASE WHEN (TPRIATV.IDEFX = ? OR ? = 0) THEN TGFITE.QTDNEG ELSE 0 END) AS QTDNEG  	FROM TGFITE INNER JOIN TGFCAB ON (TGFITE.NUNOTA = TGFCAB.NUNOTA) 					INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT CODPROD, CONTROLE, DTVAL FROM TGFEST) TGFEST ON (TGFEST.CODPROD = TGFITE.CODPROD AND TGFEST.CONTROLE = TGFITE.CONTROLE) 					INNER JOIN TPRROPE ON TGFCAB.NUNOTA = TPRROPE.NUNOTA 					INNER JOIN TPRIATV ON (TPRIATV.IDIATV = TPRROPE.IDIATV AND TGFCAB.IDIPROC = TPRIATV.IDIPROC) 	WHERE TGFCAB.IDIPROC = ? AND TGFITE.SEQUENCIA > 0  	AND TGFCAB.TIPMOV <> 'F'  GROUP BY TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX  UNION  SELECT TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL AS DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX AS IDEFX,  	   SUM(CASE WHEN TPRIATV.IDEFX != ? THEN TGFITE.QTDNEG ELSE 0 END) AS QTDNEG  	FROM TGFITE INNER JOIN TGFCAB ON (TGFITE.NUNOTA = TGFCAB.NUNOTA) 					INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT CODPROD, CONTROLE, DTVAL FROM TGFEST) TGFEST ON (TGFEST.CODPROD = TGFITE.CODPROD AND TGFEST.CONTROLE = TGFITE.CONTROLE) 					INNER JOIN TPRROPE ON TGFCAB.NUNOTA = TPRROPE.NUNOTA 					INNER JOIN TPRIATV ON (TPRIATV.IDIATV = TPRROPE.IDIATV AND TGFCAB.IDIPROC = TPRIATV.IDIPROC) 	WHERE TGFCAB.IDIPROC = ?  	AND TGFITE.CODPROD = ?   	AND TGFITE.SEQUENCIA > 0  	AND TGFCAB.TIPMOV <> 'F'  GROUP BY TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX  ORDER BY IDEFX DESC, DTVAL ASC

 SELECT TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL AS DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX AS IDEFX,  	   SUM(CASE WHEN (TPRIATV.IDEFX = ? OR ? = 0) THEN TGFITE.QTDNEG ELSE 0 END) AS QTDNEG  	FROM TGFITE INNER JOIN TGFCAB ON (TGFITE.NUNOTA = TGFCAB.NUNOTA) 					INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT CODPROD, CONTROLE, DTVAL FROM TGFEST) TGFEST ON (TGFEST.CODPROD = TGFITE.CODPROD AND TGFEST.CONTROLE = TGFITE.CONTROLE) 					INNER JOIN TPRROPE ON TGFCAB.NUNOTA = TPRROPE.NUNOTA 					INNER JOIN TPRIATV ON (TPRIATV.IDIATV = TPRROPE.IDIATV AND TGFCAB.IDIPROC = TPRIATV.IDIPROC) 	WHERE TGFCAB.IDIPROC = ?  	AND TGFITE.CODPROD = ?   	AND TGFITE.SEQUENCIA > 0  	AND TGFCAB.TIPMOV <> 'F'  GROUP BY TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX  UNION  SELECT TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL AS DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX AS IDEFX,  	   SUM(CASE WHEN TPRIATV.IDEFX != ? THEN TGFITE.QTDNEG ELSE 0 END) AS QTDNEG  	FROM TGFITE INNER JOIN TGFCAB ON (TGFITE.NUNOTA = TGFCAB.NUNOTA) 					INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT CODPROD, CONTROLE, DTVAL FROM TGFEST) TGFEST ON (TGFEST.CODPROD = TGFITE.CODPROD AND TGFEST.CONTROLE = TGFITE.CONTROLE) 					INNER JOIN TPRROPE ON TGFCAB.NUNOTA = TPRROPE.NUNOTA 					INNER JOIN TPRIATV ON (TPRIATV.IDIATV = TPRROPE.IDIATV AND TGFCAB.IDIPROC = TPRIATV.IDIPROC) 	WHERE TGFCAB.IDIPROC = ?  	AND TGFITE.CODPROD = ?   	AND TGFITE.SEQUENCIA > 0  	AND TGFCAB.TIPMOV <> 'F'  GROUP BY TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX  ORDER BY IDEFX DESC, DTVAL ASC

	(PROMP.CODPROD = ?)

	(PROPA.CODPROD = APA.CODPRODPA)
LEFT JOIN TPROEST OEST ON
	(OEST.IDEFX  IN (SELECT IDEFX FROM TPRATV WHERE IDPROC = IPROC.IDPROC))

	APO.NUAPO = ?
	AND APA.SEQAPA = ?

##ID_340## tempo: 2 (ms)
/* Runtime-info

uri: /mgeprod/service.sbr
*/
 SELECT TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL AS DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX AS IDEFX,  	   SUM(CASE WHEN (TPRIATV.IDEFX = ? OR ? = 0) THEN TGFITE.QTDNEG ELSE 0 END) AS QTDNEG  	FROM TGFITE INNER JOIN TGFCAB ON (TGFITE.NUNOTA = TGFCAB.NUNOTA) 					INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT CODPROD, CONTROLE, DTVAL FROM TGFEST) TGFEST ON (TGFEST.CODPROD = TGFITE.CODPROD AND TGFEST.CONTROLE = TGFITE.CONTROLE) 					INNER JOIN TPRROPE ON TGFCAB.NUNOTA = TPRROPE.NUNOTA 					INNER JOIN TPRIATV ON (TPRIATV.IDIATV = TPRROPE.IDIATV AND TGFCAB.IDIPROC = TPRIATV.IDIPROC) 	WHERE TGFCAB.IDIPROC = ?  	AND TGFITE.CODPROD = ?   	AND TGFITE.SEQUENCIA > 0  	AND TGFCAB.TIPMOV <> 'F'  GROUP BY TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX  UNION  SELECT TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL AS DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX AS IDEFX,  	   SUM(CASE WHEN TPRIATV.IDEFX != ? THEN TGFITE.QTDNEG ELSE 0 END) AS QTDNEG  	FROM TGFITE INNER JOIN TGFCAB ON (TGFITE.NUNOTA = TGFCAB.NUNOTA) 					INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT CODPROD, CONTROLE, DTVAL FROM TGFEST) TGFEST ON (TGFEST.CODPROD = TGFITE.CODPROD AND TGFEST.CONTROLE = TGFITE.CONTROLE) 					INNER JOIN TPRROPE ON TGFCAB.NUNOTA = TPRROPE.NUNOTA 					INNER JOIN TPRIATV ON (TPRIATV.IDIATV = TPRROPE.IDIATV AND TGFCAB.IDIPROC = TPRIATV.IDIPROC) 	WHERE TGFCAB.IDIPROC = ?  	AND TGFITE.CODPROD = ?   	AND TGFITE.SEQUENCIA > 0  	AND TGFCAB.TIPMOV <> 'F'  GROUP BY TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX  ORDER BY IDEFX DESC, DTVAL ASC

##ID_356## tempo: 3 (ms)
/* Runtime-info

 SELECT TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL AS DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX AS IDEFX,  	   SUM(CASE WHEN (TPRIATV.IDEFX = ? OR ? = 0) THEN TGFITE.QTDNEG ELSE 0 END) AS QTDNEG  	FROM TGFITE INNER JOIN TGFCAB ON (TGFITE.NUNOTA = TGFCAB.NUNOTA) 					INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT CODPROD, CONTROLE, DTVAL FROM TGFEST) TGFEST ON (TGFEST.CODPROD = TGFITE.CODPROD AND TGFEST.CONTROLE = TGFITE.CONTROLE) 					INNER JOIN TPRROPE ON TGFCAB.NUNOTA = TPRROPE.NUNOTA 					INNER JOIN TPRIATV ON (TPRIATV.IDIATV = TPRROPE.IDIATV AND TGFCAB.IDIPROC = TPRIATV.IDIPROC) 	WHERE TGFCAB.IDIPROC = ?  	AND TGFITE.CODPROD = ?   	AND TGFITE.SEQUENCIA > 0  	AND TGFCAB.TIPMOV <> 'F'  GROUP BY TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX  UNION  SELECT TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL AS DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX AS IDEFX,  	   SUM(CASE WHEN TPRIATV.IDEFX != ? THEN TGFITE.QTDNEG ELSE 0 END) AS QTDNEG  	FROM TGFITE INNER JOIN TGFCAB ON (TGFITE.NUNOTA = TGFCAB.NUNOTA) 					INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT CODPROD, CONTROLE, DTVAL FROM TGFEST) TGFEST ON (TGFEST.CODPROD = TGFITE.CODPROD AND TGFEST.CONTROLE = TGFITE.CONTROLE) 					INNER JOIN TPRROPE ON TGFCAB.NUNOTA = TPRROPE.NUNOTA 					INNER JOIN TPRIATV ON (TPRIATV.IDIATV = TPRROPE.IDIATV AND TGFCAB.IDIPROC = TPRIATV.IDIPROC) 	WHERE TGFCAB.IDIPROC = ?  	AND TGFITE.CODPROD = ?   	AND TGFITE.SEQUENCIA > 0  	AND TGFCAB.TIPMOV <> 'F'  GROUP BY TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX  ORDER BY IDEFX DESC, DTVAL ASC

##ID_381## tempo: 2 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao

uri: /mgeprod/service.sbr
*/
 SELECT TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL AS DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX AS IDEFX,  	   SUM(CASE WHEN (TPRIATV.IDEFX = ? OR ? = 0) THEN TGFITE.QTDNEG ELSE 0 END) AS QTDNEG  	FROM TGFITE INNER JOIN TGFCAB ON (TGFITE.NUNOTA = TGFCAB.NUNOTA) 					INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT CODPROD, CONTROLE, DTVAL FROM TGFEST) TGFEST ON (TGFEST.CODPROD = TGFITE.CODPROD AND TGFEST.CONTROLE = TGFITE.CONTROLE) 					INNER JOIN TPRROPE ON TGFCAB.NUNOTA = TPRROPE.NUNOTA 					INNER JOIN TPRIATV ON (TPRIATV.IDIATV = TPRROPE.IDIATV AND TGFCAB.IDIPROC = TPRIATV.IDIPROC) 	WHERE TGFCAB.IDIPROC = ?  	AND TGFITE.CODPROD = ?   	AND TGFITE.SEQUENCIA > 0  	AND TGFCAB.TIPMOV <> 'F'  GROUP BY TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX  UNION  SELECT TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL AS DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX AS IDEFX,  	   SUM(CASE WHEN TPRIATV.IDEFX != ? THEN TGFITE.QTDNEG ELSE 0 END) AS QTDNEG  	FROM TGFITE INNER JOIN TGFCAB ON (TGFITE.NUNOTA = TGFCAB.NUNOTA) 					INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT CODPROD, CONTROLE, DTVAL FROM TGFEST) TGFEST ON (TGFEST.CODPROD = TGFITE.CODPROD AND TGFEST.CONTROLE = TGFITE.CONTROLE) 					INNER JOIN TPRROPE ON TGFCAB.NUNOTA = TPRROPE.NUNOTA 					INNER JOIN TPRIATV ON (TPRIATV.IDIATV = TPRROPE.IDIATV AND TGFCAB.IDIPROC = TPRIATV.IDIPROC) 	WHERE TGFCAB.IDIPROC = ?  	AND TGFITE.CODPROD = ?   	AND TGFITE.SEQUENCIA > 0  	AND TGFCAB.TIPMOV <> 'F'  GROUP BY TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX  ORDER BY IDEFX DESC, DTVAL ASC

  3 = 12356

	(PROMP.CODPROD = ?)

	(OEST.IDEFX  IN (SELECT IDEFX FROM TPRATV WHERE IDPROC = IPROC.IDPROC))

/* Runtime-info

 SELECT ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.CODINSTPRINC, REG.TIPO FROM TGFITR ITR   INNER JOIN TGFREG REG ON (REG.CODREGRA = ITR.CODREGRA)   INNER JOIN TGFCER CER ON (CER.CODREGRA = REG.CODREGRA) WHERE   CER.TIPO = 'U'    AND CER.ATIVO = 'S'    AND ITR.ATIVO = 'S'    AND CER.CHAVE = ?    AND TRANSLATE(UPPER(REG.INSTPRINC),'\C1\C9\CD\D3\DA\C3\D5\C2\CA\CE\D4\DB\C0\C8\CC\D2\D9\C7','AEIOUAOAEIOUAEIOUC') = ?   AND CER.FILTRAR = 'S'    AND (REG.INSTSEC IS NULL OR REG.INSTSEC = '')  ORDER BY ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.SEQUENCIA
Params:
  1 = 0
  2 = PRODUTO
